IntegrateWise is one connected, Spine-powered workspace for humans and their Digital Twin. It unifies your tools, data, and AI into one governed operational layer — so context survives, humans stay in control, and continuity connects everything.
Does IntegrateWise replace Salesforce, HubSpot, or my existing tools?
No. Your systems of record stay exactly where they are. IntegrateWise sits in the middle as a coordination layer — not a replacement. The Spine unifies data from all your tools into one connected context. What you edit in IntegrateWise syncs back to your existing tools automatically.
The Spine is the connected context layer at the center of IntegrateWise. It receives normalized inputs from all connected systems and keeps your entire operational reality coherent. The Spine powers the AI — not the other way around.
Every action follows the same pattern: the system proposes, the human approves, and nothing executes without explicit confirmation. Every proposal carries evidence, confidence scores, and a full audit trail. You can review, approve, or reject any action.
Yes. Security is built into every layer. OAuth-based integrations with scoped tokens. No raw secrets stored on the client. Per-tenant data isolation. Full audit trails across lineage, approval logs, and change history. Enterprise plans include SSO and advanced access controls.
Most teams are connected within hours, not weeks. Connect your first tool in minutes. The Twin starts learning your operational reality immediately. Full governance policies can be configured within a day.
We connect to Salesforce, HubSpot, Zendesk, Slack, Gmail, Notion, Google Drive, Stripe, Jira, Asana, Airtable, and more. Custom connectors are available for Enterprise customers.
How is IntegrateWise different from Zapier or Make?
Zapier and Make move data between tools in a linear, trigger-based flow. IntegrateWise creates a persistent, governed layer that unifies data into one connected context — the Spine. It is not about moving data. It is about creating shared operational reality with memory, governance, and AI reasoning.
Yes. We offer a 14-day pilot for qualified teams. During the pilot, you connect up to 3 tools and experience the full Workbench with one Twin instance.
Your data is yours. Export everything at any time. We never hold your operational reality hostage.
Common questions about IntegrateWise: what is the Spine, how does the Twin work, pricing, and security.
